Build Setup tasks
-----------------
init - Initializes a new Gradle build.
wrapper - Generates Gradle wrapper files.

Documentation tasks
-------------------
language:lang-kotlinx:javadoc - Generates Javadoc API documentation for the 'main' feature.
language:lang-kotlinx:lang-kotlinx-test:javadoc - Generates Javadoc API documentation for the 'main' feature.
